			}

				limit = {
					is_core_of = USB
					OR = {
						has_state_category = pastoral
						has_state_category = rural
						has_state_category = village
						has_state_category = town
						has_state_category = suburb
						has_state_category = large_suburb
					}
					NOT = {
						any_neighbor_state = {
							OR = {
								has_state_category = large_city
								has_state_category = metropolis
								has_state_category = megalopolis
								has_state_category = conurbation
							}
						}
					}
				}
				decrease_state_category = yes
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
		}
	}

							building = office_park
							size > 0

						}
					}

					add_building_construction = {
						type = office_park
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = office_park
							size > 0
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = office_park
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}

		}

			}

			activate_mission = USB_insurgency_mission
			add_stability = -0.02
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_controlled_state = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = {
							modifier = USC_freedom_underground_state_dynamic
						}
						resistance > 50
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = USB_insurgency_level
					value = 2
					tooltip = add_insurgency_to_2_tt
				}
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = {
							modifier = USC_freedom_underground_state_dynamic
						}
						resistance > 50
					}
					set_state_flag = USB_insurgency_cores
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = USB_insurgency_level
					value = 1
					tooltip = add_insurgency_to_1_tt
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = USB_insurgency_cores
				}
				add_resistance = 5
			}
			random_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = USB
					is_controlled_by = USB
					OR = {
						has_state_category = pastoral
						has_state_category = rural
						has_state_category = village
						has_state_category = town
					}
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = USB_insurgency_cores
					}
				}
				set_state_flag = USB_insurgency_cores
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = USB_countryside_insurgency_state_dynamic
				}
				#remove_core_of = USB
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
					check_variable = {
						var = USB_insurgency_level
						value = 10
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = usb.107
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USB_insurgency_level
						value = 6
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = USB_event_106_flag }
					}
					country_event = usb.106
				}
				random_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = USB_insurgency_cores
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Insurgent Army\" division_template = \"Insurgent Army\" start_experience_factor = 0.15 start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
						owner = USC
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Insurgent Army\" division_template = \"Insurgent Army\" start_experience_factor = 0.15 start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
						owner = USC
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Insurgent Army\" division_template = \"Insurgent Army\" start_experience_factor = 0.15 start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
						owner = USC
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USB_insurgency_level
						value = 3
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				if = {
